/**
 * 通用统计 sdnClickNew
 * @name sdnClickNew
 * @function
 * @param key
 * @param type
 */
function sdnClickNew(num,type){
    if(!num){
        return;
    }
    var src = (new Date()).getTime();

    switch(type){
        case "aspx":
            src = 'http://sdn.kugou.com/link.aspx?id=' + num + '&url=&t=' + src;
            break;
        case "php":
        default: 
            src = 'http://tj.kugou.com/front/link.php?id=' + num + '&url=&t=' + src;
            break;
    }
    (new Image()).src = src;
}

function sdnClick(num) {
	(new Image()).src = "http://sdn.kugou.com/link.aspx?id=" + num + "&url=&t=" + Math.random();
};
function read(name, key) {
	var cookieValue = "";
	var search = name + "=";
	if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
		offset = document.cookie.indexOf(search);
		if (offset != -1) {
			offset += search.length;
			end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", offset);
			if (end == -1) {
				end = document.cookie.length;
			}
			cookieValue = document.cookie.substring(offset, end);
		}
 
	}
	var a = cookieValue.split("&");
	var o ={};
	for(var i = 0, l = a.length; i < l; i++){
		var k = a[i].split("=");
		o[k[0]] = k[1];
	}
	return o;
}
 
function login(){
	var kugouC = read("KuGoo");
	var user_name = kugouC.NickName;
	var kugou_id = kugouC.KugooID;
	var pic_src = kugouC.Pic;
	var str = "";
	var el = document.getElementById("lng");
	user_name = user_name.replace(/%/g, "\\");
	var user = eval("'" + user_name + "'");
	el.className += " logined";

    str += '<a target="_blank" href="http://www.kugou.com/job/hr/html/index.html" class="btn_zhao"></a>';
	if(!pic_src || pic_src == "default.jpg"){
		pic_src = "http://imge.kugou.com/kugouicon/165/20120724/20120724145917274529.jpg";
	} else if(pic_src.indexOf("http://") != -1){
		pic_src = pic_src;
	} else {
			pic_src ="http://imge.kugou.com/kugouicon/165/"+pic_src.substr(0,8)+"/"+pic_src;
	}
	var t= Math.random();
	str += '<a class="pic" hidefocus="true" target="_blank" hidefocus="true" href="http://www.kugou.com/newuc/user/uc/?t='+t+'"><img id="myheadpic" src="' + pic_src + '" width="32" height="32"/></a>';
	str += '<a hidefocus="true" id="mynickname" target="_blank" href="http://www.kugou.com/newuc/user/uc/?t='+t+'" class="blue">' + user + '</a> <a hidefocus="true" href="http://www.kugou.com/newuc/login/outlogin" class="logout">退出登录</span>';
	el.innerHTML = str;
	document.getElementById("link_uc").href = "http://www.kugou.com/newuc/user/uc/?t="+t;
	document.getElementById("link_uc").target = "_blank";
	try{
		loginNotice && loginNotice();
	}catch(e){}
}
/*分类统计*/
function logStat(type, name, p1, p2, p3, p4) {
		var param = [];
		type != undefined && param.push("type=" + encodeURIComponent(type));
		name != undefined && param.push("name=" + encodeURIComponent(name));
		p1 != undefined && param.push("p1=" + encodeURIComponent(p1));
		p2 != undefined && param.push("p2=" + encodeURIComponent(p2));
		p3 != undefined && param.push("p3=" + encodeURIComponent(p3));
		p4 != undefined && param.push("p4=" + encodeURIComponent(p4));
		var url = "http://log.stat.kugou.com/statistics/statistics.html?" + param.join("&") + "&t=" + new Date().getTime();
		setTimeout(function() {
			new Image().src = url;
		}, 1);
	}
/*-end- 分类统计 -end-*/

function phpLogClick(id, async) {
	async = async || true;

				(new Image()).src = "http://tj.kugou.com/front/link.php?id=" + id + "&d=" + Math.random();

		try {
			(new Image()).src = "http://tj.kugou.com/front/link.php?id=" + id + "&d=" + Math.random();
		} catch (ex) { }
	}
};

<script type="text/javascript">
	/*对联广告居中*/
	var MoveCoupletTimer = null;
	var IsBlastAdFinsh = false;
	var IsLeftCouplet = false;
	var IsRightCouplet = false;
	function MoveCoupletAd() {
		if (MoveCoupletTimer == null) {
			MoveCoupletTimer = setInterval(function() {
				Kg.$("LeftCoupletAD").style.top = document.documentElement.clientHeight / 2 + document.documentElement.scrollTop - 200 / 2 + "px";
				Kg.$("RightCoupletAD").style.top = document.documentElement.clientHeight / 2 + document.documentElement.scrollTop - 200 / 2 + "px";
			}, 100);
		}
	}
	/*对联广告加载完必*/
	function CoupletLoad(type) {
		if (type == "Left") {
			IsLeftCouplet = true;
		}
		else if (type == "Right") {
			IsRightCouplet = true;
		}
		else if (type == "blastAd") {
			IsBlastAdFinsh = true;
		}

		if (IsLeftCouplet && IsRightCouplet && IsBlastAdFinsh) {
			Kg.$("LeftCoupletAD").style.display = "";
			Kg.$("RightCoupletAD").style.display = "";
			setTimeout(function() {
				Kg.$("LeftCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "none";
				Kg.$("RightCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "none";
				Kg.$("LeftCoupletButton").style.display = "";
				Kg.$("RightCoupletButton").style.display = "";
			}, 5000);
		}
	}
	/*显示对联广告*/
	function ShowCoupletAD() {
		Kg.$("LeftCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "";
		Kg.$("RightCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "";
		Kg.$("LeftCoupletButton").style.display = "none";
		Kg.$("RightCoupletButton").style.display = "none";
		setTimeout(function() {
			Kg.$("LeftCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "none";
			Kg.$("RightCoupletBigAdFrame").style.display = "none";
			Kg.$("LeftCoupletButton").style.display = "";
			Kg.$("RightCoupletButton").style.display = "";
		}, 5000);
	}
	/*关闭对联广告*/
	function CloseCoupletAD() {
		clearInterval(MoveCoupletTimer);
		MoveCoupletTimer = null;
		Kg.$("LeftCoupletAD").style.display = "none";
		Kg.$("RightCoupletAD").style.display = "none";
	}
</script>
	<!--对联广告 start-->
    <div style="position: absolute; top: 0px; left: 15px;">
        <div id="LeftCoupletAD" style="position: relative; top: 300px; display: none;">
            <iframe id="LeftCoupletBigAdFrame" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" style="width: 80px;
                height: 160px;" onload="CoupletLoad('Left')" src="http://p.kugou.com/?id=19"></iframe>
            <img alt="酷狗广告" id="LeftCoupletButton" src="http://gg.kugou.com/mini/images/coupleCloseBtn1.gif"
                style="display: none; width: 25px; height: 160px; cursor: pointer;" onmouseover="ShowCoupletAD()" />
            <div style="cursor: pointer;" onclick="CloseCoupletAD()">
                关闭</div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div style="position: absolute; top: 0px; right: 15px;">
        <div id="RightCoupletAD" style="position: relative; top: 300px; display: none;">
            <iframe id="RightCoupletBigAdFrame" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" style="width: 80px;
                height: 160px;" onload="CoupletLoad('Right')" src="http://p.kugou.com/?id=19"></iframe>
            <img alt="酷狗广告" id="RightCoupletButton" src="http://gg.kugou.com/mini/images/coupleCloseBtn1.gif"
                style="display: none; width: 25px; height: 160px; cursor: pointer;" onmouseover="ShowCoupletAD()" />
            <div style="cursor: pointer;" onclick="CloseCoupletAD()">
                关闭</div>
        </div>

	function LoadIframe(){
		var els = document.getElementsByTagName("iframe");
		for(var i = 0; i < els.length; i++){
			if(els[i].getAttribute("_isrc"))
				els[i].src = els[i].getAttribute("_isrc");
		}
	}

	function getCommendMoreUrl(index){
		var url = "";
		switch(index){
			case 0:
				url = "http://www.kugou.com/yy/album/index/1-1-1.html";
				break;
			case 1:
				url = "http://www.kugou.com/yy/album/index/1-1-1.html";
				break;
			case 2:
				url = "http://www.kugou.com/yy/rank/commend/1.html";
				break;
		}

		return url;
	}

	}

	function getOriginalUrl(index){

				break;
		}

		return url;
	}
	
	function optSong(idx, type){
		var data = songData[type];
		if(data && data.length > 0){
			var json = [{
				"Hash":data[idx].hash,
				"FileName":data[idx].filename,
				"timeLen":data[idx].duration/1000
			}];
			//alert(Kg.JSON.stringify(json));
			KgWebSuperCall.playSongs(Kg.JSON.stringify(json), 'yueku_index');
		}
	}

	function optAllSong(type){
		var data = songData[type];
		var idx = 0;
		var count = 10;
		var files = [];
		if(type == "hy"){
			idx = t3_1.currentIndex;
			count = 10;
		} else if(type == "om"){
			idx = t3_2.currentIndex;
			count = 10;
		} else if(type == "rh"){
			idx = t3_4.currentIndex;
			count = 10;
		}  else if(type == "other"){
			idx = t3_5.currentIndex;
			count = 10;
		} else if(type == "hot"){
			idx = t7.currentIndex;
			count = 12;
		}

		for(var i = count*idx; i < count*(idx+1); i++){
			if(data[i]){				
				var json = {
					"Hash":data[i].hash,
					"FileName":data[i].filename,
					"timeLen":data[i].duration/1000
				};
				files.push(json)
			}
		}
		if(files.length > 0){
			//alert(Kg.JSON.stringify(files));
			KgWebSuperCall.playSongs(Kg.JSON.stringify(files), 'yueku_index');
		}
	}

	function play(data){
		if(data == ""){
			return;
		}

		var arr = data.split(",");
		var files = [];
		for(var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++){
			var item = arr[i];
			var param = item.split("|");
			if(param.length == 3){
				var json = {
					"Hash":param[2],
					"FileName":param[0],
					"timeLen":param[1]
				};
				files.push(json)
			}
		}
		if(files.length > 0){
			//alert(Kg.JSON.stringify(files));
			KgWebSuperCall.playSongs(Kg.JSON.stringify(files), 'yueku_index');
		}
	}

	function playAlbum(id, type){
		var url = "";
		if(type == 1){
			url = "http://www.kugou.com/yy/album/song/aid=" + id;
		} else {
			url = "http://www.kugou.com/yy/special/song/sid=" + id;
		}
		Kg.postJSON(
			url,
			{
			},
			function(res){
				if(res.status == 1 && res.total > 0){
					var files = [];
					for(var i = 0; i < res.data.length;i++){
						var json = {
							Hash:res["data"][i].hash,
							FileName:res["data"][i].singername + " - " + res["data"][i].songname,
							timeLen:res["data"][i].duration/1000
						};
						files.push(json);
					}
					if(files.length > 0){
						//alert(Kg.JSON.stringify(files))
						KgWebSuperCall.playSongs(Kg.JSON.stringify(files), 'yueku_index');
					}
				}
			},null,false
		);
	}


	function PlayMV(title,data){
		if(data == ""){
			return;
		}

		var param = {
			"filename":title,
			"mvurl":data
		};
		KgWebSuperCall.playMv(param);
	}
	function bdtongji(){//百度事件跟踪
		var addressUrl = document.location.href;
		if(/\/1153/.test(addressUrl)){//官网hao123渠道
			_hmt.push(['_trackEvent','123software', '53download', '123kugou']);
			phpLogClick(4115);
		}else if(/\/1145/.test(addressUrl)){//官网360渠道
			_hmt.push(['_trackEvent','360software', '45download', '360kugou']);
			phpLogClick(4116);
		}else{
			_hmt.push(['_trackEvent','pcsoftware', 'pcdownload', 'pckugou']);
		}

	}
	function init(){
		//根据来源不同修改PC下载ID
		var addressUrl = window.location.href,
		kg_new_download_a = Kg.$C("kg_new_download")[0].getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
		if(/\/1153/.test(addressUrl)){//官网hao123渠道
			kg_new_download_a.id = "53download";
			referrer_360_123 = true;
		}else if(/\/1145/.test(addressUrl)){//官网360渠道
			kg_new_download_a.id = "45download";
			//referrer_360_123 = true;
		}else{
			kg_new_download_a.id = "pcdownload";
		}
		//根据来源不同修改PC下载ID


		/*登录按钮添加点击事件*/
		var loginLink = Kg.$C("login")[0].getElementsByTagName('a')[2];
		var loginEvent = loginLink.onclick;
			loginLink.onclick = function(){
				loginEvent();
				phpLogClick(4544);
				return false;
			}
		t1 = new Tab("ctr", "span", "focus", "a", {
			autoPlay : true,
			timeout : 5000,
			delay:200,
			event : "mouseover"	
		});		
		
		t2 = new Tab("tab2", "span", Kg.$C("song")[0], "div",{
			event:"mouseover",
			callback:function(){
				var cidx = t2.currentIndex;
				var url = getCommendMoreUrl(cidx);
				Kg.$C("more","tab2")[0].href = url; 
			}
		})

		t3 = new Tab("sgl_song", "span", "single0", "div", {
			event:"mouseover"
		});
		
		t3_1 = new Tab(Kg.$C("single_nav","snl_song_hy")[0], "span", "snl_song_hy", "div", {
			event:"mouseover"
		});
		t3_2 = new Tab(Kg.$C("single_nav","snl_song_om")[0], "span", "snl_song_om", "div", {
			event:"mouseover"
		});
		t3_4 = new Tab(Kg.$C("single_nav","snl_song_ry")[0], "span", "snl_song_ry", "div", {
			event:"mouseover"
		});

				t3_5 = new Tab(Kg.$C("single_nav","snl_song_other")[0], "span", "snl_song_other", "div", {
			event:"mouseover"
		});
		
		t7 = new Tab(Kg.$C("single_nav","single4")[0], "span", "single4", "div",{
			event:"mouseover"
		});	
		
		t8 = new Tab("tab3", "span", Kg.$C("hot_top_10")[0], "div",{
			event:"mouseover",
			callback:function(){
				var cidx = t8.currentIndex;
				var url = getHitBillUrl(cidx);
				Kg.$C("more","tab3")[0].href = url; 
			}
		});	

		t9 = new Tab("tab4", "span", Kg.$C("hot_top_10")[1], "div",{
			event:"mouseover",
			callback:function(){
				var cidx = t9.currentIndex;
				var url = getHotBillUrl(cidx);
				Kg.$C("more","tab4")[0].href = url; 
			}
		});	
		
		new Lazyload();
		
		LoadIframe();
	}

		//CDN探针
		function cdn(domain, url) {
			var cdnimg = new Image(),
				starttime = new Date().getTime();
			cdnimg.onload = function() {
				try {
					setTimeout(function() {
						(new Image()).src = "http://dr.kugou.net/v.gif?kgdt=web_speed&type=1&time=" + (new Date().getTime() - starttime) + "&domain=" + domain + "&from=web";
					}, 0);
				} catch (ex) {}
			}
			cdnimg.onerror = function() {
				try {
					setTimeout(function() {
						(new Image()).src = "http://dr.kugou.net/v.gif?kgdt=web_speed&type=0&time=0&domain=" + domain + "&from=web";
					}, 0);
				} catch (ex) {}
			}
			cdnimg.src = url;
		}
		setTimeout(function() {
			cdn("www2", "http://www2.kugou.com/common/images/logo.jpg");
			cdn("www", "http://www.kugou.com/common/images/logo.jpg");
		}, 5000);

		! function() {
			var idc = document.createElement("script");
			idc.src = 'http://www.kugou.com/yy/static/js/idc.js?201505211743';
			idc.type = 'text/javascript';
			document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(idc);
		}();

	}
init();
